msg:The room is quite new and seems to have been renovated. The room is in a modern and comfortable style, and the hotel lobby is in an exaggerated European Baroque style. The front desk is enthusiastic and efficient, and takes the trouble to answer inquiries. The guest room aunt is polite and proactive, and delivers items to the guest room in a timely manner. The security guards at the door are well-trained and proactive in clearing the traffic flow. They warmly and politely remind car owners to drive carefully, pull over and not occupy the passage. The local business of this hotel is also very good. During the National Day, people get married almost every day. At most, there are wedding photos from three families in the lobby on one day, and three weddings are held at the same time. There is also a swimming pool and gym, which are fully equipped with five-star hardware facilities. The only shortcoming is that the breakfast room is too small, there are not enough tables, and there are too many guests. It is difficult to find a seat for breakfast at eight o'clock. The breakfast is quite satisfactory and has local characteristics. We booked this place because it has a good location and good value for money. We originally planned to stay at Ruiyi Hotel near Tengwang Pavilion. The locals suggested that it would be better for us to stay at Tai Nike in the same class as Crossing River. We found that it would cost one-third less if we stayed in Crossing River. After paying for the room, I decided to change my booking to TyNike. It was just one more stop on the subway when I went out to play. And if you want to go to Qiushui Square and Nanchang Star Ferris Wheel, it is more convenient to stay in Honggutan across the river.
